[2;36m                    [0m         [39m## Description[0m                                                                      [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m         [39mInitial issue  [0m                                                                     [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  - WRITE of size [0m[1;36m1[0m[39m at a stack address in thread T0  [0m                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  - The overflow is attributed to `mg_pfn_iobuf_private` in `printf.c` during a [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mcall chain:  [0m                                                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m    mg_pfn_iobuf_private → mg_putchar_iobuf_static → scpy → mg_vxprintf → [0m          [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m         [39mLLVMFuzzerTestOneInput  [0m                                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- The overflow target is a local buffer in `mg_vxprintf`’s stack frame: two [0m        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mtemporary arrays [0m[1;39m([0m[39m`tmp`, `tmp371`[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m of fixed size. The second buffer [0m[1;39m([0m[39m`tmp371`[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m at [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39moffsets [0m[1;39m[[0m[1;36m112[0m[39m,[0m[1;36m120[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m is overrun by one byte.  [0m                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- The error consistently reproduces on every patch attempt, confirming it is in the[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mformatting code rather than in the harness.[0m                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mPatch attempt  [0m                                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- The patch modifies `src/log.c`:  [0m                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  [0m[1;36m1[0m[39m. Replaces `#include [0m[32m"log.h"[0m[39m` with `#include [0m[32m"mongoose.h"[0m[39m` and adds `#include [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<stdlib.h>`.  [0m                                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  [0m[1;36m2[0m[39m. Inside `[0m[1;35mmg_log[0m[1;39m([0m[39mconst char *fmt, [0m[33m...[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m`, removes the original `[0m[1;35mmg_vxprintf[0m[1;39m([0m[33m...[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m`[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mcall and trailing `[0m[1;35mlogs[0m[1;39m([0m[32m"\r\n"[0m[39m, [0m[1;36m2[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m`.  [0m                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  [0m[1;36m3[0m[39m. Adds allocation of an `iobuf` structure [0m[1;39m([0m[39m`[0m[1;35mmalloc[0m[1;39m([0m[1;35msizeof[0m[1;39m([0m[39m*io[0m[1;39m)[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m`[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m, checks for [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mNULL, sets `io->len = [0m[1;36m0[0m[39m`, calls `[0m[1;35mfprintf[0m[1;39m([0m[39mstderr, [0m[32m"%s"[0m[39m, io->buf[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m`, then frees the [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mbuffer.  [0m                                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  [0m[1;36m4[0m[39m. Removes the helper function `nibble` entirely.  [0m                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- The patch is intended to bypass the static buffer logic in `mg_log` by using an [0m  [2m                [0m
